And say, "The Truth has come and the falsehood has perished. The falsehood is bound to perish
And We reveal, of the Quran, that which is a healing and a mercy to the believers. And it adds to nothing but doom of the wicked people
And when We bestow some favour on man, he keeps himself arrogantly aloof. And when anything bad happens to him, he is in despair
Say, "Every one goes his own way. And your Lord knows who it is that is guided to the right path
And they ask you about the soul. Say, "The soul is one of the commands of my Lord. And you are not given knowledge but a little thereof
And if We so will, We could certainly take away that which We have revealed to you. Then you would not find anyone to guard it for you against Our doing so
Except for Mercy from your Lord! His favour upon you is indeed abundant
Say, "Even if men and jinn should join together and help each other to bring about the like of this Quran, they would not be able to do it
And certainly, in this Quran, We have variously explained every aspect of life for mankind. But most of them did not but reject it ungratefully
And they say, "We will not believe in you until you cause a fountain to gush forth from the earth for us
Or there are for you a garden of date-palms and grape-vines with rivers flowing luxuriantly through them
Or you cause the heaven to come down upon us in pieces as you think it would, or you bring Allah and the angels before us
Or you have a house of gold, or you ascend into heaven, and we will not believe in your ascent until you bring down to us a book for us to read." Say, "Glorified is my Lord! Am I anything but a mortal man sent with a divine Message
And nothing prevented people from believing when the divine Guidance came to them except for what they said, "Has Allah raised a mortal man as His Messenger
Say, "Had angels been the normal inhabitants on earth, We would certainly have sent down to them from the heaven an angel as divine Messenger
Say, "Allah suffices as a witness between me and you. HE is indeed well aware and minutely observant of all His human creatures
And the one, whom Allah guides, is the one who is guided. And the one, whom He leaves to go astray, you shall not find any awliya for him besides Him. And We will gather them together, on the Day of Resurrection, all lying on their faces — blind, dumb and deaf. Their abode shall be in Hell. We will increase the intensity of the blazing Fire, whenever it abates, for them
This is their retribution because they suppressed the truth of Our Messages/Verses/Signs and because they said, "What! When we shall have become bones and dust, shall we then indeed be raised up as a new creation
Do they not see that Allah — Who created the heavens and the earth and appointed an end for them wherein there in no doubt — is able to create their like?hBut the wicked people do not but suppress the Truth
Say, "Even if you were in control of the treasures of the Mercy of my Lord, you would miserly hold on to it for fear of exhausting it. And man is stingy
And We did give Moses nine clear signs. Ask the Children of Israel about them. When he came to them, Pharaoh told him, "I do indeed consider you, O Moses, to be a man bewitched
Moses said, "You do know that none but the Lord of the heavens and the earth has sent down these as clear evidence. And I do indeed consider you, O Pharaoh, to be a man doomed
Then Pharaoh wanted to get them destabilised in the land. And We drowned him and those with him all together
And, afterwards, We said to the Children of Israel, "Settle down in the land. Then when the second prophecy would come to pass, we will bring you together in one place
And in truth have We sent itdown, and in truth has it come down. And We have not sent you but as the giver of good news and as a warner
And We have made divisions in the Qur'aan and sent it down in stages, so that you recite it to the people at intervals
Say, "Believe in it or not; but they indeed, who are given the knowledge before it, fall down on their faces in humble prostration, when it is recited to them
And they say, "Glorified is our Lord! The prophecy of our Lord was bound to be fulfilled
And they fall down on their faces weeping, and it adds to their humility
Say, "Pray to Allah or pray to the Gracious One; you may pray to Him by any of His beautiful names. And say your ritual prayer neither too loudly nor in an undertone, but choose a suitable tone in between
And say, "To Allah is due all praise, Who has taken no son to Himself. And He has no partner in His absolute sovereignty, and has no infirmity to protect against. And do proclaim His greatness
All praise is due to Allah, Who sent down the Book to His devotee and made it flawless
That shall remain immutable and straight so that it might warn them of severe punishment from Him and give good news to the believers, who do good deeds, that they shall have a good reward (Paradise)
They (the believers) shall stay therein for ever
And warn those who say, "Allah has a son
They know nothing of it, nor did their fathers know. A grave word it is that comes out of their mouths! They speak nothing but a lie
Then maybe you (Prophet) will kill yourself with grief, on their account, if they do not believe in this Pronouncement (Qur'aan)
We have indeed made whatever is on the earth as an adornment for it, and We put them on trial to see which of them do good deeds
And We will indeed turn everything thereon into barren soil
Did you perchance consider the Men of the Cave and the story about them as among Our extraordinary signs
When the youths sought refuge in the cave, they said, "Our Lord! Grant us mercy from Thee, and facilitate for us the right course in our affair
So We put a seal on their ears for a number of years in the cave
Then We raised them up to see which of the two groups was best able to compute the time they had remained there in their unconscious state
We relate to you their story in truth. They were indeed youths who believed in their Lord and We favoured them with more guidance
And We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and said, "Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth. We pray not to any god besides Him; for, then, certainly, we would have uttered an abominable thing
These, our people, have taken gods besides Him! Why do they not produce any clear evidence in their support? Is there, then, anyone committing a greater wrong than one who concocts a lie against Allah
And when you leave them and what they worship besides Allah, go to the cave for refuge. Your Lord will extend His mercy to you and facilitate ease in your affair
And you would see the sun bypass their cave, as it rose in the morning on the right; and as it declined in the afternoon on the left, it would pass them by while they lay in the spacious space in the cave. This is one of the signs of Allah. The one whom Allah guides, is the one rightly guided, and the one whom He misleads, you shall not find for that one any wali to direct him to the right path
And you might think them awake, but they were asleep. And We made them turn to the right side and to the left, and their dog squatted on its outstretched forelegs at the entrance. Had you come upon them you would certainly have run away from them, and you would certainly have been overwhelmed with fear of them
And so We roused them to make enquiries among themselves. One of them asked, "How long have you been here?" They said, "We have been here for a day or less than a day." Some said, "Your Lord alone knows how long you have been. Now send one of you with this silver coin of yours to the city, and let him find and bring some good food for you. And let him ensure that none comes to know about you
For indeed if they should find you out, they would stone you to death or force you back into their religion. And, then, you will never get salvation
And thus We made people to stumble upon them (the Men of the Cave) that they (people) might know — when they quarrelled among themselves in their affair — that Allah's promise is true and that there is no doubt about the Hour. And they (the people who came to know the story of the Men of the Cave) said, "Erect a monument over them." Their Lord is well aware of them. Those who had authority over people's affairs said, "We will certainly raise a place of worship over them
Some of the people would later say, "They (the Men of the Cave) were three, the fourth being their dog." and some others would say, "Five, the sixth being their dog," making conjectures about what is unknown. And still others would say, "Seven, and the eighth was their dog." Say, "My Lord knows their number. None but a few know it. So argue not about them except for what you do know, and make no enquiries concerning them with any of the people
And never say about anything, "I will indeed do it tomorrow
Without adding, "If Allah pleases." And remember your Lord when you forget and say, "Maybe my Lord will guide me to better conduct than this
And they remained in their cave for three hundred years and some add nine to the number
Say, "Allah knows how long they remained. To Him belong secrets of the heavens and the earth. HE sees them and He hears! There is no walih for them besides Him, and He does not share His Sovereignty with any one
And recite what has been revealed to you of the Book of your Lord! There is none who can alter His words. And you shall find no provider of shelter besides Him
And be yourself patient with those who pray to their Lord, morning and evening, desiring His good pleasure. And let not your eyes stray away from them, desiring glamour of life in this world. And follow not him whose heart We have made neglectful to Our remembrance and who follows his carnal desires and is reckless in his deeds
And say, "This is the truth from your Lord. So he who wants to, let him believe, and he who wants to, let him suppress the Truth." We have indeed prepared for those who indulge in wrong-doing a fire, the flames of which shall encompass them. And if they cry for help, they shall be given water like molten brass which will scald their faces. What a miserable drink and what a miserable resting-place
We shall indeed not let the reward, of those who believe and do good, go waste
These it is for whom are gardens of perpetuity beneath which rivers flow. Reclined comfortably on decorated couches, they will be adorned therein with bracelets of gold, and they will wear green robes of fine silk and heavy brocade. What an excellent reward and how beautiful a resting place
And tell them the parable of two men. For one of them We made two gardens of grape vines, and We bordered them both with date-palms. And between the two gardens We made cornfields
Each of the gardens yielded its fruits, and nothing went wrong therein. And We caused a spring to gush forth in their midst
And he had good yield. So he said to his companion in a conversation with him, "I have more wealth than you, and I command greater respect among the people
And he entered his garden; and he was unfair to himself. He said, "I do not think that this will ever perish
And I do not think the Hour will ever occur. And even if I am returned to my Lord I will certainly find there a better place than this
His companion answered, "Do you deny Him Who created you from dust, then from a tiny seed of fertilized ovum and then shaped you into a man
But as for me, He, Allah, is my Lord, and I do not associate anyone with my Lord
And why did you not say when you entered your garden that it is as Allah has willed and that there is no power but with Allah? If you see me inferior to you in wealth and children
Then maybe my Lord will give me something better than your garden, and send a thunderbolt from heaven on your garden so that it shall become just a barren land
Or its waters should sink deep into the ground so that you are unable to find it
And the yield of his gardens was caught in a disastrous wave of destruction. And he started wringing his hands for his investments therein, which had turned upside down. And he said, "Alas! I should not have associated anyone with my Lord
And he had no manpower to help him besides Allah, nor could he help himself
There! Allah is the only True Wali. He is best in giving rewards and the best to go to in the end
And tell them that the life of this world is like water which We send down from the sky. Spring forth therewith all kinds of vegetation on the earth. Then it (vegetation) becomes dry and brittle and the winds scatter it. And Allah has the ability to do all things
Wealth and children are but an adornment of the life of this world. And the abiding good deeds are better, for reward and hope, with your Lord
And on the Day when We will cause the mountains to move away and you will see the barren earth, We will gather them and leave none of them behind
And they shall be lined up before your Lord. "Verily, you have come to Us in the state We created you at first. But you had thought that We had not fixed any appointment for you
And the Book shall be produced. And you will see the sinners scared of its contents. And they will say, "Oh, woe to us! What a book is this! It omits nothing, small or big, but mentions them all." And whatever they had done, they shall find it there. And your Lord causes no wrong to anyone
And when We asked the angels to prostrate to Adam, they all did prostrate, but Iblees did not! e was a jinni, and he swerved from the commandment of his Lord. Would you then take him and his progeny, rather than Me, as awliya, and they are your enemies? What a miserable exchange for the wrongdoers
I did not make them witness the creation of the heavens and the earth, nor of the creation of their own selves. And there was no question of my taking those who mislead as helping hands
And on the Day when He shall say, "Call those whom you considered to be My associates!" So they shall call them, but they shall not respond to them. And We shall place a destructive barrier between them
And the sinners shall see the Fire, and they shall know that they are going to fall into it. And they shall find no way out therefrom
And We have certainly explained in this Quran, for the benefit of mankind, examples of every kind. And man is, in most things, quarrelsome
And nothing prevents people from believing and asking forgiveness of their Lord — when the guidance has already come to them — except that what happened to the ancient peoples should overtake them or that the punishment should confront them
And We do not send Messengers but as givers of good news and of warnings. And those who suppress the Truth resort to falsehoods that they may extinguish the truth thereby. And they hold My Verses/signs and warnings in ridicule
And who is worse in wickness than he who is reminded of the Verses/signs of his Lord, but turns away therefrom and forgets what his two hands have sent before ? We have indeedh placed covers over their hearts, and deafness in their ears, lest they should understand it (Lord's Verses/signs). And if you call them to guidance, they will not follow it ever
And your Lord is Forgiving, full of Mercy. Was He to catch them for what they earn, He would certainly have hastened the punishment for them. But there is an appointed time for them from which they shall find no escape
And these towns We destroyed when they acted unjustly — We had fixed an appointed time for their destruction
And when Moses said to the youth accompanying him, "I will not stop until I reach the confluence of two rivers even if I have to continue this journey for a long time
So when they reached the confluence, they forgot their fish, and it burrowed its way into the sea
But when they had gone farther, he said to his young companion, "Take out our breakfast. We have certainly met with fatigue in this journey of ours
The youth said, "You know when we took some rest on the rock, I forgot about the fish — and nothing but the Satan made me forget to tell you about it — when, strangely, it found its way into the river
Moses said, "That was the spot we had sought for!" They then retraced their footsteps back to the spot
There they found one of Our devotees. We had favoured him with mercy from Us and We had given him some knowledge from Us
Moses said to him, "May I follow you so that you teach me of the right knowledge you have been taught
He said, "You can never have patience with me
And how can you have patience in matters over which you do not have comprehensive knowledge
He said, "Allah willing, you shall find me patient and I shall not disobey you in any matter
He said, "If you would follow me, question me not about any thing until I myself speak to you about it
And both of them went out on a journey. And there arose no problem between them until when they boarded a boat he (Moses' new companion) made a hole in it. Moses said, "Have you made a hole in it to drown the people thereon? Certainly you have done a grave thing
Moses' companion said, "Did I not say that you will not be able to have patience with me
Moses said, "Hold me not responsible for a thing I forgot, and burden me not with difficulty in my affair
And they both went on until, when they met a boy, he (Moses' companion) killed him. Moses said, "Have you killed an innocent person otherwise than for manslaughter? Certainly you have done a condemnable thing
Moses' companion said, "Did I not tell you that you will not be able to have patience with me
Moses said, "If I ask you about anything after this, keep me not in your company. Verily, you shall have then an excuse, provided by me, for you to do so
And they both went on until, when they came to a town, they requested its people to give them some food, but they refused to feed them as guests. They then found in it a wall which was about to collapse and Moses' companion set it right. Moses said, "You could certainly have taken some wages for it
Moses' companion said, "This shall be the parting between me and you. I will now inform you of the true perspective of my actions over which you could not have patience
As for the boat, it belonged to some poor men who worked on the river. And I wished to make it defective as there was, across them, a king who seized every boat by force
And as for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared lest he should trouble them with disobedience and ingratitude
So we desired that their Lord would give them in his place a boy better than him in purity and more compassionate
And as for the wall, it belonged to two orphaned boys in the city, and there was beneath it a treasure belonging to them, and their father was a righteous man. So your Lord desired that they should attain their maturity and take out their treasure as a mercy from your Lord. And I did not do it of my own accord. This is the true perspective of my actions over which you could not have patience
And they ask you about Zulqarnain. Say, "I will recite an account of him to you
We did indeed give him authority on earth and means to pursue any thing he did
So he followed a means
And when he reached a place as the sun declined in the west, he found it declining on a oligotrophic spring. And he found a people living near it. We said, "O Zulqarnain! Cause them to suffer or treat them well
He said, "We will punish only the one who is wicked. He shall then be returned to his Lord, and He will punish him with a severe punishment
And as for him who believes and does good deeds, he shall have good reward, and We will make Our command easy for him
Then he followed another means
And when he reached a place as the sun rose in the East, he found it rise on a community to whom We had given no shelter therefrom
And thus We had put a limit to the knowledge he (Zulqarnain) could have
Then he followed yet another means
And when he reached a place between two mountains, he found beyond these a people who could hardly understand a word
They said, "O Zulqarnain! Gog and Magog do indeed make mischief in this land. May we then give you expenses so that you raise a barrier between us and them
Zulqarnain said, "What my Lord has given me is better than what you would give me. So you assist me with labour only and I will construct an obstruction between you and them
Bring me iron sheets." And when he had filled up the gap between the two mountain sides, he said, "Blow!" And when he had turned it red hot, he said, "Bring me molten brass to pour over it
So they were not able to scale it nor could they breach it
He said, "This (construction of the barrier/gate) is a mercy from my Lord. But when the prophecy of my Lord comes to pass, He will level it to the ground, and the prophecy of my Lord has ever to come true
And, one day, We shall let the different communities of mankind get mixed up with one another like waves.And then the trumpet will be blown, and We shall gather them all together
And We shall present the Hell, that Day, for display before those who had suppressed the Truth
— Those whose eyes had a cover against seeing My Reminder (Qur'aan) and who were unable to listen to it
Do they then who suppress the Truth think that they can take My subjects as awliya, besides Me? We have indeed prepared Hell as the destination of those who suppress the Truth
Say, "Shall We inform you who the greatest losers are in their deeds
They are those whose efforts in the life of this world are misdirected and they think that they are doing good work
Those are the people who suppress the Truth in the Verses/signs of their Lord and of the appointment with Him. So their deeds have become null and void. And so We will not assign any weightage to their deeds on the Day of Resurrection
That Hell is their recompense because they suppressed the Truth and held My Verses/signs and My Messengers in ridicule
For those who believe and do good deeds, their bestowal shall indeed be the gardens of paradise
They will abide therein; they will never seek any transfer therefrom
Say, "If the sea were ink for the words of my Lord, the sea would surely be exhausted before the words of my Lord are exhausted, though We were to bring the like of it (sea) in aid
Say, "I am only a man like you. It is revealed to me that the Entity you should worship is One and Only. So, whoever hopes to meet his Lord, he should do good deeds, and worship none besides his Lord." h
About such initials at the beginning of certain Chapters, please see study note : (Manzil I)
This is a narration of the mercy of your Lord on His devotee Zachariah
When he prayed to his Lord silently
He prayed, "My Lord! My bones have indeed become weak and my head shining white. And, my Lord! I have never been disappointed in my prayer to You
And indeed I worry about what my relatives will do after me. And my wife is barren. So bestow upon me a proper heir from You
Who shall be an heir to me and an heir to the children of Jacob. And make him, my Lord, one in whom You are well pleased
[The divine response was,] "O Zachariah! We do indeed give you the good news of a boy whose name shall be Yahya (John). We had not given this name to anyone before
Zacharia said, "O my Lord! How can I have a son, and my wife is barren, and I have myself grown too old
[The divine response was,] "So shall it be. Your Lord says, `It is not at all difficult for Me, and indeed I created you before, when you were nothing
Zachariah said, "My Lord! Give me a sign." The Lord said, "Your sign is that you will not be able to speak to the people for three consecutive nights
So he came out to his people from the chamber, then he communicated to them, through signs, that they should glorify Allah morning and evening
O John! Hold on to the Book firmly." And We granted him the authority over men while he was yet a child
And We gave him the gift of compassion from Us and of purity, and he feared Allah
And ever courteous to his parents, he was never insolent, disobedient
And peace on him on the day he was born, the day he dies, and the day he is raised to life again
And mention Mary in the Book when she withdrew from her family to stay at a place towards the East
And she screened herself from them, and We sent to her Our spirit, and it appeared before her as a man well-made
She said, "I do indeed seek the Gracious Allah's protection against you, if you do really fear Allah
He said, "I am a Messenger of your Lord: I am sent to give you a gem of a boy
She said, "How can I have a boy when no man has ever touched me? And I have never been unchaste
He said, "It will be so even in those circumstances — Your Lord says, `It is easy for Me.' — so that We may make him a sign for men, and a mercy from Us. And it is a matter which has already been decreed
So she conceived him and then withdrew with him to a remote place
And the throes of childbirth drove her to the trunk of a palm tree. She said, "Oh, would that I had died before this, and had been a thing long forgotten
Then a voice called out to her from beneath her, "Grieve not, your Lord has surely made a canal flow beneath you
And shake the trunk of the palm tree towards you. It will drop on you fresh ripe dates
So eat and drink and relax! Then if you should see any man, tell him (by signs), "I have indeed vowed unto the Gracious Allah not to speak to any man today
And she came to her people carrying the child. They said, "O Mary! You have verily done a terrible thing
O sister of Aaron ! Your father was not a bad man, nor was your mother an unchaste woman
But she pointed to him. They said, "How could we speak to a mere child in cradle
The child said, "I am indeed a devotee of Allah. HE has given me the Book and made me a Prophet
And He has made me blessed wherever I may be, and He has enjoined on me prayer and charity so long as I live
And to be couteous to my mother. And He has not made me insolent, impudent
And peace on me on the day I was born, the day I die and the day I am raised to life again
This (as narrated in Verses to above) then is Jesus, son of Mary — the word of Truth about which they raise disputes
It is not befitting the majesty of Allah that He should beget a son. Glorified He is! When He has decreed a matter, He only says to it "Be," and it is
And, indeed, Allah is my Lord and your Lord; hence, worship Him. This is the Straight Path
But the tribes disagreed among themselves — and woe to those who disbelieve — about the Court of Judgment to be assembled on a tremendous Day
Make them listen to you when you speak to them about the Day they shall appear before Us, and make them understand the significance of that Day. But those who are wicked shall continue to remain grossly mistaken about the Day
And warn them of the Day of intense regret, when all matters get finally decided. And they are under a delusion and they do not believe
We do indeed inherit the earth and all those who are on it, and to Us they all shall be returned
And make mention of Abraham in the Book. He was indeed a true Prophet
When he said to his father, "O my father! Why do you worship a thing that neither hears nor sees, nor does it give you any benefit whatsoever
O my father! I do have some knowledge that you do not. So follow me! I will show you the Right Path
O my father! Worship not the Satan. The Satan is indeed a rebel against Allah, the Gracious
O my father! I am afraid, a punishment from the Gracious Allah may afflict you and you may befriend the Satan
He (Abraham's father) said, "Are you averse to my gods, O Abraham? If you do not desist I will certainly pelt you with stones. And leave me alone for now
Abraham said, "Peace on you! I will pray to my Lord to forgive you. He is indeed ever benevolent to me
And I will go away from you and what you pray to besides Allah, and I will pray to my Lord; may be my prayer to my Lord shall not remain unanswered
So when he had gone away from them and what they worshipped besides Allah, We bestowed upon him Isaac and Jacob, and We made each a Prophet
And We bestowed upon them Our mercy, and We gave them each a highly truthful tongue
And mention Moses in the Book. He was indeed pure and clean; and he was a Messenger Prophet
And We called to him from the right side of Mount Sinai, and We drew him near for a talk
And We made for him, by Our mercy, his brother Aaron a Prophet
And mention Ishmael in the Book. He was indeed true to his word, and a Messenger Prophet
And he used to enjoin his family to pray and to give in charity, and his Lord was well pleased with him
And mention Idris in the Book. He was indeed a true Prophet
And We raised him high in status
Those were men on whom Allah bestowed favours. Those were from among the Prophets of the seed of Adam, and of those whom We carried in the Ark with Noah, and of the seed of Abraham and Israel, and of those whom We guided and chose. Whenever Verses/signs of the Gracious Allah were recited to them, they would fall down prostrating and weeping
But then generations that followed them became negligent of prayers and followed sensual desires. And they shall encounter disaster
Except such as repent and believe and do good deeds. These shall enter the Garden, and no injustice shall be done to them
Gardens of perpetuity which the Gracious Allah has promised to those who worship Him even when they do not see Him. His promise shall indeed come to pass
They shall not hear therein any vain discourse; the discourse shall be only on peace. And they shall have all their provisions therein morning and evening
This is the garden that We cause those of Our subjects to inherit who fear Allah
And we (angels) do not descend but by the command of your Lord. To Him belongs whatever is before us and whatever is behind us and whatever is in between. And your Lord does not forget
The Lord of the heavens and the earth and what is in between them. So worship Him and be patient in worshipping Him. Do you know any one equal to Him
And says man, "When I am dead and gone, shall I even then certainly be brought out alive
Does not man remind himself that We had created him before, when he was nothing
And, by your Lord, We will most certainly gather them and the satanic people together. Then shall We certainly cause them to be present around Hell on their knees
Then We will most certainly pull out from every group one who had transgressed most against Allah, the Gracious
And We do certainly know best those who deserve most to be burned therein
And there is not one of you, but shall come to it. For your Lord this is a decree already issued
And We will save (from Hell) those who fear Allah, and We will consign the wrongdoers therein on their knees
And when Our clear Verses/signs are recited to them, those who disbelieve say to those who believe, "Which of the two groups of us are better in position and well organised
And how many of the generations have We destroyed before them who were apparently well established
Say, "The Gracious Allah will surely give a long lease to all those who have gone astray, until they see what they were warned about: the punishment or the Hour. Then they shall know who is worse in position and weaker in force
And Allah increases guidance of those who go by the Guidance. And lasting good deeds are better for reward with your Lord and yield better return
Have you, then, seen him who suppresses the Truth in Our Verses/signs and says, "I shall certainly be given wealth and children
Has he gained knowledge of the unseen, or made a pact with the Gracious Allah
By no means! We write down what he says, and We will extend the duration of the punishment for him
And We will inherit from him what he talks of (his wealth and his children), and he shall come to Us alone
And they have taken gods, besides Allah, as sources of power for them
By no means! They shall soon deny their worshipping them, and they shall be adversaries to them
Do you not see that We have sent the devils against those who suppress the Truth, inciting them on in their pernicious deeds
So be not hasty about them. Their days are numbered
The Day on which We shall gather before Allah, the Gracious, groups of pious people
And We will drive the criminals in herds towards Hell
They shall have no power of intercession, unless one has struck a deal with the Gracious One
And they say, "The Gracious One has a son
Certainly you have come up with an atrocious thing
The heavens almost were torn asunder thereat, the earth was disturbed, and the mountains collapsed devastatingly
At that they ascribed a son to the Gracious One
And it is inconceivable that the Gracious One could have a son
None in the heavens and the earth but will come to the Gracious One obediently as a slave
Certainly He has counted them and He has given everyone a number
And all of them will come to Him, individually, on the Day of Resurrection
Allah will certainly create affection for those who believe and do good deeds
And then We have made it (the Qur'aan) easy in your tongue only so that you may give good news thereby to those who fear Allah and warn thereby a hostile people
And how many a generation before them have We destroyed! Do you have any perception of any of them or hear any sound from them
Ta-ha
We have not sent down the Quran upon you to cause you distress
It is but a Memorandum for one who fears Allah
It is a bestowal from the One Who created the earth and the lofty heavens
From the Gracious One, firmly established on the throne of absolute authority
Everything — that which is in the heavens, on the earth, in between the two, and underneath the ground — is all His
And if you say anything aloud, mind you, He knows the secret, and the hidden
Allah — there is no god but He; His are the very best attributes
And has Moses' story come down to you
When he saw some fire, he said to his wife escorting him, "Wait! I do indeed see a fire. Maybe, I can bring to you therefrom a live burning coal or come to know about the right way from someone at the fire
And when he came to it (the fire), he was called out, "O Moses
Verily, I am your Lord; so take off your shoes! You are indeed in the sacred valley of Tuwa
And I have chosen you, so then listen to what is revealed
Indeed, I, Myself, am Allah! There is no god but I. So worship Me and establish regular prayer to remember Me
The Hour (Last Day) is indeed coming. I will unravel it anytime so that every soul is recompensed for what it strived
So let him not, who does not believe in it (the Hour) and follows his low desires, turn you away from it so that you should perish
And what is this in your right hand, Moses
Moses said, "It is my staff. I lean upon it and I beat the leaves with it to make them fall upon my sheep, and I have other uses for it
Allah said, "Cast it down, O Moses
And as Moses cast his staff down, it instantly became a serpent moving
Allah said, "Hold it and be not afraid! We will restore it to its original state
And, another sign: put your hand under your arm, it shall come out perfectly white
That We may show you some of Our great signs
Go to Pharaoh! He has indeed exceeded all bounds
He said, "O my Lord! Broaden my mind for me
And make my task easy for me
And correct the stammer in my speech
Make them understand what I say
And appoint, from my family, an assistant for me
My brother, Aaron
Strengthen me with his support
And make him my associate in my work
So that we should glorify You much
And remember You often
You do indeed see us
Allah said, "Your petition stands granted, O Moses
And We did confer a favour on thee another time
When We revealed to your mother that which was revealed
That she should put him into a chest, and then put the chest onto the river. Then the river should throw him on the shore. There, one, who is an enemy to Me and enemy to him, should pick him up. And I made you lovable so that you might be brought up under My watchful eye
When your sister went and said, `May I lead you to one who will feed him?' Thus We returned you to your mother so that she should be comforted and not grieved. And you killed a man, and then We delivered you from that worry. And We tried you variously. Then you stayed for years among the people of Madyan. Then you came here as ordained, O Moses
And I have made you for Myself
Now go, you and your brother, with My signs and be not remiss in remembering Me
Go both of you to Pharaoh! He has indeed committed transgression
And speak to him gently. Maybe he takes heed or refrains from further evil
Both said, "O our Lord! We do indeed fear that he may take no heed of us or that he may commit some transgression
Allah said, "Fear not! I, Myself, am indeed with you both; I hear and I see
So go you both to him and say, `We two are, indeed, Messengers of your Lord. Send the Children of Israel with us and torment them not! Verily, we have brought to you a sign from your Lord. And peace on him who follows the guidance
It has indeed been revealed to us that punishment will come upon him who rejects and turns away
Pharaoh asked, "And who is the Lord of you two, O Moses
Moses said, "Our Lord is He Who gave everything its creation, and then guided it
Pharaoh asked, "Then what about the earlier generations
Moses said, "The knowledge thereof is in a record with my Lord. My Lord errs not, nor does He forget
The Lord Who made the earth for you a flattened expanse and laid for you therein paths. And He sent down water from the sky. Then thereby We have brought out diverse herbs/plants in pairs
Eat and tend your cattle. There are indeed signs in this for those who are prudent
From it (earth) We created you and into it We shall send you back and from it will We raise you a second time
And verily We showed him Our signs, all of them, but he rejected and turned arrogant
Pharaoh said, "Have you come to drive us out of our land by your magic, O Moses
We shall certainly then bring to you similar magic. Let us then, between us and you, have an appointment at a mutually convenient place, which we should neither of us fail to keep
Moses said, "Let your appointment be on the day of the Festival and let the people be gathered together in the morning
So Pharaoh withdrew, devised his plan of action, and then came
Moses said to them, "Woe to you! Do not fabricate a lie against Allah, lest He should destroy you by a punishment. And he, who fabricates, does indeed fail
And the magicians debated among themselves their response to Moses, but kept the discourse secret
They said (among themselves), "Indeed, these two are just magicians. They wish to turn you out of your land by their magic and to deprive you of your best traditions
So do combine your plan, and then come in line. And he that is superior will certainly win this day
They said (aloud), "O Moses! Will you do your act, or shall we be the first to do it
He said, "No! You do it." And lo! Their ropes and their sticks appeared to him (Moses), by their magic, as if they were moving
So Moses felt a fear rising within him
WE said, "Fear not, you shall indeed have the upper hand
And cast down that which is in your right hand. It shall devour what they have contrived. They have contrived only what a magician could plan. And the magician shall not succeed wherever he may have come from
And the magicians were obliged to fall prostrate! They said, "We believe in the Lord of Aaron and Moses
Pharaoh said, "You believed in him before I gave you leave. He ought to have been your superior who taught you magic. I will then certainly cut off your hands and your feet from opposite sides, and I will certainly crucify you on the trunks of the palm trees. And certainly you will come to know which of us is the more severe and the more persistent in punishing
The magicians said, "There is no question of our preferring you over Him Who made us, after what has come to us of clear signs. So decide whatever you want to. You can only decide about life in this world
We do indeed believe in our Lord. May He forgive us our sins and that magic which you forced upon us. And Allah is better and everlasting
Whoever comes to his Lord as a sinner, for him indeed is Hell. He shall not die therein, nor shall he live
And whoever comes to Him as a believer with righteous deeds to his credit, he shall be among those who shall enjoy high ranks
Gardens of perpetuity, beneath which rivers flow, to abide therein. And this is the reward of one who purifies oneself
And We did reveal to Moses that he should "travel by night with My devotees, then make for them a dry path in the sea, without any fear of being overtaken or of any other sort
And Pharaoh followed them with his armies. And so there came upon them from the sea that which came upon them
And Pharaoh led his people astray and guided them not
O Children of Israel! We did verily deliver you from your enemy, and We made a covenant with you on the right side of the mountain, and We sent to you the manna and the quails
Make use of the good things We have provided you with, and be not inordinate therein lest My wrath should become due upon you. And he, upon whom My wrath becomes due, certainly perishes
And I am indeed most forgiving to him who repents and believes and does good deeds, and then follows the right direction
And what made you come here earlier than your people, O Moses
Moses said, "They are close behind me. And I hastened to You, my Lord, that You might be pleased
Allah said, "But then We put your people on trial after you had left them behind, and the Samiri has led them astray
Then Moses returned to his people, angry and sorrowful. He Said, "O my people! Did not your Lord give you a good promise? Did then the time for fulfillment of the promise seem too long to you? Or did you wish to incur wrath from your Lord, so you broke your promise to me
They said, "We did not break our promise to you of our own accord, but we were made to bear the burden of the ornaments of the people. So we got rid of that burden just as the Samiri did
Then he (Samiri) brought out for them a body of a calf, from which emanated a low sound. Then he told them, "This is your god and the god of Moses. But he (Moses) has forgotten it
Could they not see that it did not respond to them at all, and that it did have no power to do any harm or to bring any benefit to them
And certainly had Aaron told them earlier, "O my people! You are only being tried therewith. And, indeed, your Lord is the Gracious One. Follow me then and obey my order
They had said, "We will not abandon worshipping it until Moses returns to us
Moses said, "O Aaron! What prevented you, when you saw them going astray
From following me? Did you then go against my instruction
Aaron said, "O son of my mother! Seize me not by my beard and by my head. I was indeed afraid you might say, `You have caused a rift among the children of Israel and not waited for my word
Moses then asked, "What have you to say on this, O Samiri
He said, "I saw what they did not see. And I took a handful of traces from the messenger and flung it. And this is what my own self prompted me to do
Moses said, "Begone! Indeed, it is ordained for you in this life to say, `Touch me not!' And indeed there is a prediction for you that shall not fail. And look at your god that you hovered around! We will certainly burn it. Then we will certainly reduce it to dust and scatter it in the sea
None but Allah is worthy of your worship! He knows everything
Thus do We narrate to you some stories from the past. And We have verily given you the account (in the Qur'aan) from Ourselves
One who turns oneself away therefromhshall indeed bear a burden on the Day of Resurrection
Burdened they shall remain. And too bad for them the burden, On the Day of Resurrection
The Day, the trumpet is blown — the Day, We gather the sinful, blue with fear
Whispering among them, "You stayed but ten days
We know best what they say; and the one among them, with the exemplary method of giving estimates, would say, "You stayed but a day
And they ask you about the mountains. Say, "My Lord will pull them down to their roots
And reduce it to a smooth, levelled plain
You shall not see therein any ups and downs
That Day they shall follow the caller, and they shall have no alternative but to follow him. And the voices shall be low in deference to the Gracious One and you shall not hear but a soft murmur
That day no intercession shall benefit anyone except from him whom the Gracious One permits and whose word of intercession He approves
HE knows what they are aware of, and what they are not aware of, and what is beyond the sphere of their knowledge
And the faces shall be bent down before the Living, Everlasting One. And he who bears the burden of wrongdoing is certainly doomed

And We said, "O Adam! This is an enemy to you and to your wife; so let him not drive you both out from the garden and thus make you miserable
It is indeed ordained for you that you shall not be hungry therein nor be naked
And that you shall not be thirsty therein nor shall you feel hot
Then the Satan seduced him, saying, "O Adam! Shall I show you the tree of immortality and a kingdom that shall not decay
And they both succumbed to the satanic seduction, and then their sexuality got opened to them, and they both began to cover themselves with leaves of the garden. And Adam disobeyed his Lord and thus deviated from the right path

He will say, "My Lord! Why have You raised me blind? And I was certainly one able to see
Allah will say, "Just as Our Verses/signs came to you but you neglected them, so shall you be neglected this day
And thus do We recompense him who is negligent and believes not in the Verses/signs of his Lord. And certainly the punishment in the Hereafter is severe and abiding
Do they not take a lesson from the fact that We had destroyed many a generation before theirs, in whose dwelling-places they now move about? Indeed, there are signs in this for those who are prudent
And had it not been that the Word had already gone forth from your Lord and an appointed term fixed, the same fate (of destruction in this world) that the earlier generations met with, would certainly be theirs (the generation addressed to in this Verse) too
Exercise patience then over what they say. And glorify your Lord with His praise before the rising of the sun and before its going down. And glorify Him, during the night and during parts of the day, so that you get peace of mind
And covet not that — which We have provided some couples among them with — of the glitter of this worldly life, whereby We try them. And what the Lord provides you with is better and lasting
And enjoin prayer on your followers, and be regular and steadfast thereon. We do not ask you for any provision; We give it to you. And in the end it is those who fear Allah, and abide by His instructions, that get all the good things to enjoy

No aspect of divinity comes to them from their Lord in the form of a fresh anecdote but they listen to it in jest

HE knows what they know of and what they do not know of. And they intercede not except for him whom He wills and they are on their guard in awe of Him

If you are in doubt about the Resurrection, then — to make things clear to you — We did indeed create you from dust, then from a little seed of fertilized ovum, then from a leech-like clinging clot of curdled blood, then from a chewed-like lump of flesh (foetus) with formed and unformed parts. Allah has promised to those of you who believe and do good deeds that He will most certainly give them the authority to rule in the earth on His behalf as He had given those before them the authority. And Allah has further promised that He will most certainly establish for them their religion which He has chosen for them, and that He will most certainly change their sense of fear with the sense of security. Let them just worship Me, and not worship any other being/thing besides Me. And whoever suppresses the Truth after this, such are the ones that transgress/rebel/pervert/profligate
And establish the prescribedh prayer and give the Zakathand obey the Messenger, so that mercy may be shown to you
Think not that those who suppress the Truth shall escape (from Allah) on the earth. And their abode is the Fire. And evil certainly is that destination
O you who believe! Let those whom your right hands possess (slaves/servants) and those of you who have not attained to puberty ask permission of you three times: before the Morning Prayer, whenever you take off your clothes (for rest) at noon, and after the Evening Prayer. These are three times of privacy for you. No restriction on you or on them at other times. Some of you have to be around others. Thus does Allah make clear to you the Verses, and Allah is Knowledgeable, Wise
And when children among you reach the age of puberty, let them seek permission as those (who had reached the age of puberty) before them sought permission. Thus does Allah makeh clear to you His Verses, and Allah is Knowledgeable, Wise
And it is no sin for women advanced in age — who do not hope for a marriage — to put off their clothes without displaying their beauty/charm. And if they restrain themselves it is better for them. And Allah hears, knows
There is no question of any blame on the blind, the lame, the sick, or you yourselves that you eat from your houses, or your fathers' houses or your mothers' houses, or your brothers' houses, or your sisters' houses, or your paternal uncles' houses, or your paternal aunts' houses, or your maternal uncles' houses, or your maternal aunts' houses, or houses you possess the keys of, or your friends' (houses). You incur no sin that you eat together or separately. So when you enter houses, greet one another with a blessed and good salutation from Allah. Thus does Allah make clear to you the Verses so that you understand these properly
Those only are believers who believe in Allah and His Messenger. And when they are with him (Messenger) on a community matter they go not away until they ask him for permission. Indeed, they who ask for your permission are the ones who believe in Allah and His Messenger. So when they ask for your permission for some personal work, give them permission at your discretion and pray to Allah for their forgiveness. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving, Merciful
Make not the Massenger's call among you to be like your call to one another. Allah indeed knows those who slip away surreptitiously from among you. So then let those who go against his counsel beware lest a trial or a painful punishment afflict them
Beware! To Allah certainly belongs everything that is in the heavens and the earth. Surely, He knows your condition. And the Day when they will be brought back to Him, He will inform them of what they did. And Allah knows all things
Blessed is He who has sent down the Criterion [Qur'aan] to His Devotee that he/it may serve as a warner to the worlds
Blessed is He to Whom belongs the the absolute sovereignty over the heavens and the earth, He Who has begotten no children and has no partner in His sovereignty. It is He Who has created every thing and it is He Who has given it its role
And yet they have taken, besides Him, deities who create nothing and they themselves are created, and who have no power to harm or benefit themselves and who who have no power over death, life, or Resurrection
Those who suppress the Truth say, "This is only a self- concocted lie and others have helped him in concocting it." Verily, then, they have perpetrated an injustice and a falsehood
And they say, "Fables of the ancients! He has had written these down which then are rehearsed to him morning and evening
Say, "HE has sent it down Who knows every secret that is in the heavens and on the earth. He is indeed Forgiving, Merciful
And they say, "What kind of a Messenger is this who eats food and roams in the marketplaces!? Why has no angel been sent down with him to warn us
Or no treasure been sent down to him, or no garden been provided to him from which to eat?" The wrongdoers further say, "You are not following but a man bewitched
See what kind of attributes they expect you to have. They have thus gone astray and cannot find the right way
Blessed is He who can give you, if He wills, better things than that: gardens under which rivers flow. And He can provide palaces for you
But they deny the Hour. We have prepared a blazing Fire for those who deny the Hour
When it (the Fire) sees them from afar, they will hear it raging and roaring
When they are thrown into a narrow space therein, chained together, they will plead for destruction (death, so that they become oblivious to their suffering in the Fire)
Plead not this day for a single destruction, but plead for many
Ask, "Is this better, or the Paradise of immortality which the pious/righteous have been promised? It is their reward and their destination
They shall forever have therein for them all that they desire. This is a promise frequently asked for of your Lord
On the Day He gathers them together with those they worship besides Him, He will ask, "Did you mislead these people whom I had created to worship Me, or did they stray away by themselves
They will say, "Your Holiness! It was not proper for us to choose any of the awliya other than You. But You gave them and their fathers the comforts of this life so much that they forgot the Remembrance (of You and Your Message, the Qur'aan) and thus became a people doomed
They have certainly then given the lie to all your pleas and you can neither ward off punishment nor get any help. And whoever of you has committed evil, he/she shall be made by Us to taste great punishment
We had not sent any Messengers before you who did not eat food and roam the market- places. We test some of you with others, whether you exercise patience. And your Lord monitors all things
And those who do not expect a meeting with Us say, "Why are angels not sent down to us or why do we not see our Lord?" They are certainly too proud of themselves and have greatly exceeded all bounds
There will be no good tidings for the guilty on the day they see the angels. And they will cry out for an invincible partition between them and the angels
And We shall proceed to turn all that they did into scattered dust
The inhabitants of the Garden will have the best abode and the finest place of rest on that Day
On a Day when the sky will split open with its clouds and the angels after angels are sent down
Sovereignty on that Day shall return defacto and dejure to the Gracious One. And it will be a hard Day for those who suppress the Truth
On that Day, the transgressor will bite his hands and say, "Would that I had walked the Messenger's path
Oh would that I had never chosen such-and-such as my friend
He made me stray away from Your Message after it had reached me. And the Satan is betrayer of mankind
And the Messenger will say, "O my Lord! My people did indeed treat this Qur'aan as a thing abandoned
And thus did We make to every prophet an inimical front from among the sinners; but your Lord is sufficient as Guide and Support
Those who suppress the Truth say, "Why was the Qur'aan not sent down to him all at once?" We did send it down thus so that We imbue your mind therewith. And We have arranged it in good order
No sooner do they come up with a problem than We bring you the truth behind and the best solution
Those who will be dragged headlong into Hell shall have an evil place to dwell in — and they had strayed away from the Right Path
And We did give Moses the Book, and made his brother Aaron his assistant
We then told them both to go to the people who had denied Our signs. We then put those people to ruin
And We drowned the people of Noah when they rejected the Messengers and We made an example of them (the people) for all mankind. And We have prepared a painful punishment for the transgressors
For AAad, Thamood, and the people of al-Rass, and for many a generation between them
To every one of them We gave warning examples and every one of them We put to annihilation
And they must have certainly come upon the town/village on which had rained down an evil rain. How could they not have seen it? Yet they have no faith in the Resurrection
Whenever they see you, they hold you not but in contempt, saying, "Is this the one Allah has sent as His Messenger
Indeed, he would almost have led us away from our deities, had we not stood firmly with them!" And when they experience the punishment, they shall realize who it is that had strayed from the path
Have you seen one who has taken one's own desire to be one'a god? Can you be a guardian over such a one
Do you think most of them can hear or understand? They are nothing but like cattle. Nay, they are those astray from the Path
Have you not observed how your Lord stretches the shadow? Had He pleased, He could have made it stationary. And We made the sun a guide over it
Then We withdraw it (shadow) to Us, an easy withdrawal
And it is He Who has made for you the night as mantle, the sleep for repose, and the day for rising
It is He who sends the winds as heralds bearing good news of His ensuing mercy and We send down pure water from the sky
We send down water so that We may bring life to a dead land and slake the thirst aplenty of Our creations of cattle and mankind
And We do distribute it (rainfall) among them so that they are gratefully aware thereof, but most of mankind respond not but in ingratitude
And if We had so willed, We would have certainly raised someone to warn, in every town/village
Do not yield then to those who suppress the Truth, but counter them strenuously by means of this [Qur'aan]
It is He who has facilitated two seas to flow and meet — one palatable and sweet and the other salty and bitter — and set up a barrier and an invincible partition between them
And He it is who has created a human being from water and then made him a link in the human relationships by blood and marriage. And your Lord is all powerful
Yet they worship besides Allah others that can neither benefit nor harm them. And the suppressor of the Truth does ever turn his back on his Lord
And We have not sent you (Prophet Muhammad) but to give good news to those who believe in Allah and abide by His Guidance given in the Qur'aan and to warn those who believe not
Say, "I do not ask you for anything in return for this except that anyone who so wishes should take the Right Path to his Lord
And have trust on the Living [Allah] Who never dies, and glorify Him with His praise. And He is well conversant with the sins His subjects commit
It is He who created the heavens and the earth, and all besides that is in and around them, in six periods of time. HE then ascended the Throne of absolute power and authority. HE is the Gracious One. Do ask any informed person about Him
When they are told to prostrate before the Gracious One, they ask, "Who is this Gracious One? Are we to prostrate to whatever you order us?" And it increases their aversion
He is the bestower of blessings who has set constellations in the heavens, as also a lamp (sun) and a moon that give light (for the inhabitants of this earth)
And He it is who has made the night and the day succeed each other — for the one who would ponder or be grateful
And human beings obedient to the Gracious One are those who walk on earth with humility and when the ignorant speak to them, they say, "Peace
And who spend the night for their Lord, lying down and standing.h
And who say, "Our Lord! Ward off from us the punishment of Hell. Its punishment is indeed atrocious
Indeed, it is an evil abode and an evil position to be in
And they (human beings obedient to the Gracious One) are those who are neither spendthrift nor miserly, but keep to a position in between
And who invoke no deity besides Allah, nor kill anyone whose killing, without due authority, Allah has prohibited, nor indulge in extramarital sexual intercourse. And whoever does this, he/she commits a sin
He/she shall have his suffering doubled on the Day of Resurrection and shall remain humiliated therein forever
But for those who repent, believe, and do good deeds, Allah will change their evil deeds into good ones. And Allah is forgiving, merciful
And the one who repents and reforms, he/she then has indeed turned to Allah in repentance
And they (human beings obedient to the Gracious One) are those who do not give false evidence, and when they pass by frivolity, they pass by with dignity
And who, when reminded of the Verses/signs of their Lord, do not stumble upon them, deaf and blind
And who say, "Our Lord! Give us joy in our wives and our children and make us exemplary for the righteous
These are the ones who will be rewarded with high position because of their endurance. They will be welcomed therein with greetings and salutations of peace
They shall live there forever — the best place to reside in and the best position to be in
Say, "Why would my Lord care for you, if you do not pray to and invoke Him? Verily then you have rejected the Truth. So soon shall the inevitable happen

And when your Lord called out to Moses: "Go to those wicked people
Go to the people of Pharaoh! They fear not (the inevitable consequence of being wicked)
Moses said, "My Lord! I do indeed fear they may not believe me
And my heart is straitened and my tongue not fluent. So then send this command to (my brother) Aaron
And, they have a criminal charge against me, so I fear they will kill me
Allah said, "Worry not about it! Go then to them, both of you, with Our signs/messages. We shall indeed be with you, ever listening
And when, both of you, come before Pharaoh, tell him, `We are indeed sent by the Lord of the worlds
So you let the children of Israel go with us
Pharaoh said, "Did we not bring you up amongst us as a child? And did you not spend among us years of your life
And you did what you did, and you remain ungrateful (that we have not punished you)
Moses said, "I did it while I was among those who go astray
And I fled from you because I feared you. And then my Lord bestowed me with a command and made me one of the Messengers
And is this a favour you did me — that you had enslaved the children of Israel
Pharaoh said: "And who is `Lord of the worlds
Moses replied, "Lord of the heavens and the earth and of all that is between them, if you would but be convinced
Pharaoh said to those around him: "Do you hear
Moses continued, "Your Lord, and Lord of your forefathers
Pharaoh interjected, "Indeed, your `Messenger' who has been sent to you is certainly mad
Moses went on, "Lord of the east and the west and of all that is between the two if you would but understand
Pharaoh Said, "Verily, if you have any deity other than me, I shall certainly put you into prison
Moses said, "Even if I bring to you clear evidence
Pharaoh said, "Produce it, then, if you are a man of truth
Moses then threw down his staff, and it became a veritable serpent
And he drew out his hand, and it appeared white to the beholders
Pharaoh said to the chieftains around him: "Indeed, this one is certainly an expert magician
He wants to drive you out of your land by his black magic. What, then, do you advise
They said, "Defer the decision on him and his brother, and send callers to cities and towns
They will bring to you all expert magicians
And so the magicians were assembled for public show at a set time on a certain day
And the people were asked, "Are you all gathered here
So that we might cheer the magicians if it is they who prevail
So when the magicians came, they said to Pharaoh, "Are we not indeed entitled certainly to a reward if it is we who prevail
Pharaoh said, "Of course! And, indeed, in that case you shall be among those who are near to me
Moses said to them: "Cast down whatever you were to cast
Then they did cast down their ropes and their staffs, and said, "By Pharaoh's honour, behold, it is we certainly who shall prevail
And then Moses threw his staff. And lo! It swallowed up all their deceptions
And the magicians fell down in prostration
They said: "We believe in the Lord of the worlds
The Lord of Moses and Aaron
Pharaoh said, "You believe him before I permit you? Indeed, he must be your master who has taught you magic! But you shall certainly come to know who the master is. I shall certainly cut off your hands and your feet on opposite sides, and shall certainly crucify you, all together
The magicians said, "No matter! We shall indeed return to our Lord
We do indeed ardently desire that our Lord forgive us our faults now that we have been among the foremost to believe
And We conveyed to Moses Allah's instructions, "Leave with My devotees (Children of Israel) by night. You will he pursued (by Pharaoh's army)
And then Pharaoh sent heralds to all cities/towns
These [Children of Israel] are but a small gang
And they have surely enraged us
And we are indeed a vigilant multitude
And so We made them (Pharaoh's people) come out of gardens and springs
And We made them (Pharaoh's people) leave their treasures and places of honour
And [in course of time] We made the Children of Israel inheritors of such things
Then they [Pharaoh's men] went in pursuit of them (Children of Israel) eastwards
Then as the two groups of people (Moses' and Pharaoh's) came in sight of each other, Moses' people exclaimed: "We are indeed certainly overtaken
Moses said, "No! My Lord is with me. HE will guide me
We then inspired Moses to strike the sea with his staff. The sea thereupon parted, and each part appeared like a vast mountain
And We drew the other party (Pharaoh's people) near thereto
And We saved Moses and all who were with him
And then We drowned the others
Therein indeed was a sign. And yet most of them would not believe
And, indeed, your Lord is certainly the One Omnipotent, Merciful
And recite to them the story of Abraham
When he asked his father and his people, "What is it this that you worship
They said, "We worship idols, and we bow down to them in devotion
Abraham asked, "Do these hear you when you invoke them
Or do they give you any benefit or any harm
Abraham's people said, "But we found our forefathers doing the same
Abraham asked, "Have you, then, ever considered what it is that you have been worshipping
You and those ancient forebears of yours
And, indeed, these are enemies to me, but not the Lord of the worlds
The Lord Who created me and Who then has guided me
And Who gives me food and drink
And, when I fall ill, Who cures me
And Who will cause me to die and then will bring me back to life
And Who, I hope, will forgive me my faults on the Day of Judgment
My Lord! grant me wisdom, and put me with the righteous
And create a good name for me among the later generations
And place me among those who shall inherit the garden of bliss
And forgive my father! He is indeed among those who have gone astray
And put me not to shame on the Day of Resurrection
The Day on which neither wealth will be of any use, nor children
Except for a mind free of evil with which one comes before Allah
And the Garden (Paradise) will be brought near for those who had spent their worldly lives within the parameters laid down by Allah
And the Hell will be laid open before those who had allowed themselves to be seduced
And they will be asked: "Where are those you worshipped
Those, other than Allah, you worshipped? Can those be of any help to you or to themselves
They will then be hurled into hell — they, as well as those who had seduced them
And the army of Iblees (the Satan) - all together
They will, blaming one another, say
By Allah, we were indeed certainly in clear delusion
When we deemed you equal to the Lord of all the worlds
And they who led us astray are none but the culprits
And now we have none to intercede for us
We have no anxious friend either
If only we had a return [to worldly life], so we could be among the believers
There is indeed a sign in this, and most of them believe not
And, indeed, your Lord — He alone — is the Omnipotent, the Merciful
The people of Noah did not believe the Messengers
When their brother Noah said to them, "Are you not scared of wrongful living
I am indeed a trustworthy Messenger of Allah sent to you
Be, then, afraid of Allah, and obey me
And no reward whatever do I ask of you for it: my reward rests with none but the Lord of the worlds
Be afraid of Allah then, and obey me
They said, "Are we to believe you, when those who follow you are the most abject of people
He said, "And what do I know what work they do
It is for none but Allah to make them account for what they do, if you could but understand this
And I am not one to drive away the believers
I am but a plain warner
They said, "If you desist not, O Noah, you will certainly be stoned to death
Noah said, "My Lord! Indeed, my people do not believe in me
Do settle then the matter between me and them, and save me and those of the believers who are with me
We then saved him and those with him in the fully-laden Ark

Helped you with cattle and children

And no reward whatever do I ask of you for it: my reward rests with none but the Lord of the worlds
Will you be left secure among things here
Amidst gardens and springs
And fields, and palm-trees with slender stalks
And do you skillfully hew dwellings out of the mountains
Be afraid of Allah then, and obey me
And obey not the command of those given to excesses
Those who spread corruption on earth and strive not to set things right

And have fear of Him who has created you, as also the generations past

So they disbelieved him. And thereupon punishment gripped them on a gloomy day. And, verily, it was a punishment of a dreadful day
There is indeed in this a sign, and most of them believed not

Upon your mind, [O Muhammad], so that you may be among those who warn
In the language of plain Arabic

And had We sent it down upon any non-Arab
And had he recited it to them in his own language, they would not have believed in it
We have likewise caused this Message to pass through the minds of those who are lost in sin
They will not believe in it (the Message) till they see the grievous punishment
That (punishment) will come upon them all of a sudden, without notice
And then they will say, "Could we have some respite
Do they, then, wish to hasten Our punishment
Do you see that if We do allow them to enjoy for years
And thereafter that which they were promised befalls them

And never have We destroyed any community without being warned
And reminded. And We wrong not
And the devils had not brought it (the Message) down

And put your trust in the Omnipotent, the Merciful
Who sees you standing
And Who sees what goes on in your mind while you are among those who prostrate before Him
He is indeed the One Who hears, the One Who knows

They descend upon all sinful turncoats
They (the devils) pass on hearsays to them (sinful turncoats). And most of them (the devils) lie
And the seducers follow the poets
Do you not see that they (poets) roam about passionately in every valley
And that they say what they do not do
Save those who believe, do righteous deeds, and remember Allah much. And they avenge themselves only after having been wronged and to the extent they are wronged.And those who do wrong will soon come to know how evil a turn they will turn to

It contains guidance and glad tidings for the believers
Those who establish prayer, give Zakaat, and believe in the Hereafter with conviction
Those indeed who do not believe in the Hereafter — We have made their deeds appear good to them, and so they stumble blindly on
It is them that the worst of punishment is reserved for. And it is they who shall be the losers in the Hereafter

When Moses said to his family, "I do indeed see a fire. I shall bring you from there some information, or bring you a burning brand so that you warm yourselves therewith
Then, when he came to it, he was called out and told, "Blessed is all that is in the fire and around it! And glory to Allah, Lord of the worlds
O Moses! It is indeed Me, Allah — the Almighty, the Wise
And throw your staff down!" Then he saw it (staff) stir as if it were a serpent. And he took to flight and did not look back! "O Moses! Fear not. The Messengers need have no fear in My Presence
Nor those need fear who do wrong and then after a bad deed they change for the good. for, indeed, I am Forgiving, Merciful
And put your hand into your pocket: it will come out blemish-less white — [these are] among nine signs unto Pharaoh and his people. They are indeed a depraved people
So then when Our clear-cut signs came unto them (Pharaoh and his people), they said, "This is pure magic
And, though their minds were convinced of their genuineness, they wickedly and arrogantly refused to accept those as signs. And behold what happened in the end to those corrupt people
And We did grant knowledge to David and Solomon. And they both said, "Praise to Allah! HE has favoured us above many of His believing devotees
And Solomon inherited David. And he said, "O people! We have been taught the speech of the birds, and have been given all kinds of things. This, indeed, is certainly a manifest favour
And Solomon's armies — of Jinns&, of human beings, and of birds — were assembled and then they were led forth in orderly ranks before him
The parade went on till, when they came upon a valley of ants, an ant said, "O ants! Get into your homes (holes), lest Solomon and his armies crush you unknowingly
Solomon then smiled broadly at her (the ant's) words, and said, "My Lord! Make me grateful for your favours which You have bestowed on me and on my parents. And make me do righteous deeds which You are pleased with. And put me in the list of Your righteous devotees
And he (Solomon) inspected the rank of the birds, and said, "How come I do not see the Hudhud ? Or is he among the absentees
I will punish it severely or slaughter it unless it brings me a convincing excuse
And when the bird registered its presence before long, it said, "I have covered something which you have not. And I have come to you from Sheba with reliable information
I did indeed find there a woman ruling over them. And she is endowed with everything. And she has a huge throne
And I found her and her people prostrating to the sun instead of to Allah! And the Satan has made their deeds look good to them, and has thus hindered them from the Right Path. And so they do not tread that Path

And when the word gets fulfilled about them, We shall bring out for them a creature from the earth, which will tell them that mankind had no real faith in Our Verses/signs. @ @ My undedrstanding of this Verse is that it applies to modern man's unabashed gobbling up of the theory of evolution. Protagonists of this theory assert that mankind evolved itself from lower forms of life through processes of natural selection and survival of the fittest. They reject the Qur'aanic assertion that a Super-intelligent, Omniscient and Omnipresent Being has consciously, deliberately or purposefully created mankind and everything else in the Universe. The thought of such a Creator is anathema for the atheists subscribing to the theory of evolution. This theory could well be the creature spoken of in this Verse, telling those who believe in it that they have no real faith in the Qur'aanic Verses/signs.
