They take cover of their oaths to turn others away from Allah's Path. It is indeed evil what they do
That is because they believe, and then suppress the Truth! Consequently, a seal has been set on their minds so that they can no longer understand
And when you see them, their body language impresses you. And when they speak, you do listen to what they say. As if they were propped up puppets! They think that every cry is [directed] upon them. They are the real enemies, so beware of them! Allah's curse be on them! How very false are they
And when they are told, "Come, Allah's Messenger will pray to Allah that you be forgiven", they shake their heads! And you see them turning arrogantly away
It is all the same for them whether you pray that they be forgiven or you do not pray; Allah will not forgive them! Allah does indeed not give guidance to the transgressors
It is they who say, "Do not spend anything on those who are with Allah's Messenger, until they break away from him." And Allah's are the treasures of the heavens and the earth. But the hypocrites do not understand this truth
They say, "If we do return to the City, the honourable ones will surely drive out therefrom the downtrodden!" And all honour belongs to Allah, and to His Messenger, and to those who believe. But this, the hypocrites do not know
O you who believe! Let not your wealth or your children distract you from remembrance of Allah. And if any do that — it is they, they who are the ones doomed
And spend out of what We have provided for you, before the death approaches any of you, and that one then says, "My Lord! If only You would give me a little more time, so that I could pay due Sadaqah and be among the righteous
But Allah does not give a human being more time when his term expires. And Allah is well aware of what you do
Everything that is in the heavens and the earth glorifies Allah. His is the Sovereignty and His, the praise. And He is the One able to do anything
He is the One Who created you. Then there are those of you who suppress the Truth and those who believe! And Allah sees what you do
He created the heavens and the earth and was His sole right to create. And He gave you shape and then made your shapes good. And to Him is the final destination
He knows all that is in the heavens and the earth, and He knows what you conceal and what you reveal. And Allah is aware of what is in the minds
Has not the history of those who suppressed the Truth in the past, and then tasted the consequences of their conduct, reached you? And a painful punishment is in store for them
That is because their Messengers (from Allah) had come to them with clear signs, but they said, "Shall a mere human guide us?" So they suppressed the Truth and turned away! And Allah is in no need of anyone or anything. And Allah is Self-sufficient, Embodiment of Praise
Those who suppress the Truth opine that they will not be raised again to life after death. Say, "Yes, verily, and by my Lord, you will be raised again! And then you will be told what you had done. And that is easy for Allah
So believe in Allah and His Messenger and the light [Qur'aan] which We have sent down. And Allah is well aware of what you do
The day He gathers you for the Day of Assembly [Resurrection], that will be a day of mutual disillusion. And he who believes in Allah and does good deeds, He [Allah] will efface his evil deeds from his account and admit him to Gardens underneath which rivers flow. Such people will abide therein for ever. That is the highest success
And those who suppress the Truth and reject Our Verses/signs — they shall be inmates of the Fire. They shall abide therein. And it is a bad end to any journey
No calamity befalls save by Allah's leave. And he who believes in Allah — He [Allah] guides his mind. And Allah knows all things
And obey Allah and obey His Messenger ! But if you turn away, then the responsibility on Our Messenger is only to convey the Message plainly
Allah — there is no god save Him. And in Allah, then, let the believers put their trust
O you who believe! There indeed are enemies to you among your wives and your children. So beware of them! And if you forgive and overlook and seek Allah's forgiveness for them, then Allah is indeed Forgiving, Merciful
Your wealth and your children are objects of trial only, for you. And with Allah there is a great reward
So fear Allah as best you can! And listen to, and obey, and spend on what is good for you! And one who is protected against stinginess of one's own self — such are the ones truly successful
If you lend a good loan to Allah, He will double it for you and will forgive you! And Allah is Appreciative of gratitude, Kind
[Allah is] Knower of the Invisible and the Visible, the Omnipotent, Wise
O Prophet! When any of you men divorce your wives, divorce them with regard to their waiting period. And keep proper count of the period, and fear Allah, your Lord. Drive them not out of their homes [during the waiting period], nor should they themselves leave unless they openly commit an immoral act. And these are the bounds set by Allah. He who transgresses Allah's bounds, wrongs himself. You never know, Allah may well bring about some new situation after that
Then when their waiting term gets over, either retain them [as wives] honourably or part with them in fair manner. Call to witness two reliable men from among you and keep your testimony upright for Allah. This admonition is given to one who believes in Allah and the Last Day. And one who fears Allah, He will make for him a way out [of his difficulties]
And Allah will provide for him [who fears Him] from an unexpected source. And one who puts his trust in Him — Allah suffices for that one. Allah does indeed bring to fruition what He decrees. He has surely set a measure for all things
And, if you have any doubt in the case of those of your wives who have either passed the age of menstruation or [for any other medical reason] not menstruating, their waiting period is three months. The waiting period of those who are pregnant is until they deliver their burden [give birth]. Allah makes His Decrees easy for those who fear Him
That is the Decree Allah has sent down to you. He who fears Allah, he shall have his evil deeds effaced from him and the reward enriched for him
Allow the women [undergoing a waiting period] to live the same way you yourselves live as per your means. And harass them not to make their lives difficult. If they are pregnant, bear their expenses until they deliver. If they suckle your infants, pay them for it. Discuss things among yourselves honestly and honourably. And if you cannot bear with each other, let another woman suckle the infants for you
May man of means spend in accordance with his means. And may him, with restricted resources, spend in accordance with what Allah has given him. Allah burdens not any person with more than what He has given him. Allah will soon bring about ease after hardship
And how many a village/town did haughtily disregard the Decree of its Lord and His Messengers? And We sternly took it to account and punished it severely
So it [village/town] tasted the evil consequences of its conduct; and its conduct ended in ruin
Allah has prepared a severe punishment for them. So, O men of understanding, who believe, fear Allah! Surely, Allah has sent down to you a Reminder [the Qur'aan]
[Through] a Messenger who conveys to you Allah's clear Verses, so that he might take those, who believe and do good deeds, out of darkness into light. Allah will admit the one who believes in Him and does good deeds into Gardens underneath which rivers flow, where such people will remain forever. Allah has surely made excellent provision for such a one
It is Allah who created the seven heavens and, of the earth, the like thereof. He sends His Decree down among them, so that you may know that Allah has power over all things, and that He does encompass all things with His knowledge
O Prophet! Why do you make unlawful what Allah has made lawful to you, seeking pleasure of your wives? And Allah is Forgiving, Merciful
Allah does enjoin upon you to deal with your oaths properly. And Allah is your Lordh Supreme, and He is the One Knowledgeable, Wise
And the Prophet once told something in confidence to one of his wives. She then divulged it [to another wife]. And Allah made this known to him. He [the Prophet] let her know a part of it [what Allah had told him] and he wit eld a part. And no sooner he let her know partially what Allah had told him, she asked, "Who has told you this!?" He replied, "The One, Knowledgeable and Aware of everything, has told me
Would that you two [Prophet's wives concerned in this episode] turn to Allah in repentance, for the minds of both of you are so inclined! And if you help each other against him [the Prophet, know that] Allah Himself is his Protector, and [consequently] Gabriel, all the righteous among the believers, and all the other angels will then come to his aid
Were he [the Prophet] to divorce you, Allah might well give him in your stead spouses better than you — women who surrender themselves to Allah, truly believe in Him, devoutly obey His will, turn to Him in repentance, worship Him alone, and who are dedicated — be they previously married or virgins
O you who believe! Shield yourselves and your families from Fire that is fuelled by human beings and stones and guarded by Angels awesome and severe. They [the Angels] do not disobey Allah in whatever He commands them, and they do whatever they are ordered to do
O you who suppress the Truth! Make no excuses today [Resurrection Day]. You are only being recompensed [this Day] for what you had been doing [in the world]
O you who believe! Turn to Allah in sincere repentance. It may well be that your Lord will efface from you your bad deeds, and will admit you into gardens underneath which rivers flow on a Day on which Allah will not put the Prophet, and those who believe with him, to any shame. Their light will run ahead of them, and on their right. They will pray, "O our Lord! Make this light of ours shine for us forever, and forgive us our sins. YOU do indeed have power over all things
O Prophet! Wage a struggle against [any bad influence or deed from] the suppressors of the Truth and the hypocrites, and deal strictly with them. And [if they do not repent,] their abode shall be Hell — and how vile a journey's end
For those who suppress the Truth, Allah gives examples of the wives of Noah and Lot. They were under two of Our righteous subjects, and each betrayed her respective husband. And so, neither [of the two husbands] would be of any avail to the two women when they would be told [on Judgment Day], "Enter the Fire with all the other entrants therein
And for those who believe, Allah gives example of Pharaoh's wife as she prayed, "My Lord! Build for me a mansion close to you in the Paradise. And save me from Pharaoh and his deeds, and save me from all evil people
And Mary, daughter of Imran! She guarded her chastity, and We breathed into it of Our spirit. And she was testimony to the truth of her Lord's words and His Books. And she was one of those totally devoted to Allah
Blessed is He in Whose hand is the Sovereignty! And He has power over all things
The One Who has created the death and the life to test which of you is good in conduct. And He is the One Omnipotent, Forgiving
The One Who has created seven heavens one over another. You shall not see anything amiss in the creation of the Gracious One! Then look again: can you see any incongruities
Then look again and yet again, your sight will return to you humbled and tired
And verily We have adorned the heaven near [the earth] with lamps [stars and planets], and We have made it a stonewall for the devils [beyond which they cannot proceed]. And We have prepared for them punishment of the blazing Fire [Hell]
And for those who suppress their belief in their Lord there is the punishment of Hell. And it is a bad journey's end
When they are flung therein they hear it roar as it boils up
As if it [Hell] would burst with rage! Whenever a crowd [of wicked people] is thrown therein the wardens thereof ask them, "Had not anyone come to warn you
They say, "Yes, verily, a warner did come to us, but we refused to believe him and said, `Allah has not sent down anything, you are not but under a great delusion
And they say, "Had we but listened or had sense, we would not now have been among the dwellers in the blazing Fire
So they acknowledge their sins! And so the dwellers in the blazing Fire are done away with
Those who fear their Lord without seeing Him — for them is forgiveness and a great reward
And whether you conceal your opinion or proclaim it, He [Allah] does indeed know all that is in the minds
Would He not know what He created!? And He is the One Subtle, Aware
He it is Who has made the earth subservient to you, so walk through its winding paths and eat of what He has provided for. And to Him will the Resurrection be
Are you sure that One in the heaven will not cause the earth to swallow you while it is in a state of convulsion
Or are you sure that the One in the heaven will not let loose on you a hurricane? But you shall soon know how terribly true My warning was
And verily those before them refused to believe! And how severe in effect was My forsaking them
Do they not see the birds above them spreading and folding their wings? Holds them up none but the Gracious One! HE does indeed look to all things
Who is it — other than the Gracious One — that will be like an army to help you out? Those who suppress the Truth are labouring under nothing but illusion
Who is it that will provide for you if He should wit old His provision? Nay, but they are given to pride and aversion
Is he who walks falling on his face [stumbling] better guided, or he who walks upright on a straight road
Say, "He it is who has brought you into being, and has endowed you with the hearing, the sights and the intellect. But you are seldom grateful
Say, "He it is Who multiplied you on the earth, and to Him you shall be gathered
And they ask, "When will this promise be fulfilled, if what you say is true
Say, "That knowledge is only with Allah, and I am but a plain warner
Then as they see it close to them [in the Hereafter], the faces of those who suppress the Truth will be distraught, and it will be said to them, "This is what you had been asking for
Say, "Do you see, whether Allah causes me (Muhammad) and those with me to perish or He bestows mercy upon us, [it is His Will?]. But, then, who will protect those who suppress the Truth from a painful punishment!?"h
Say, "He is the Gracious One. In Him we believe and in Him we put our trust. And you will soon know who is clearly astray
Say, "Do you see if your waters should sink deep into the ground, who then could bring you flowing water
Noon By the pen, and by what they write
By your Lord's grace, you [Prophet Muhammad] are not mad
And, indeed, a never ending reward is there for you
And, indeed, you have a truly great character
Soon you will see, and so they will
As to who of you is on trial
Your Lord does indeed know who has strayed from His Path, and He knows those on right guidance
Obey not then those who deny the Truth
They want you to compromise and then they will compromise
And obey not any mean swearer of oaths
Or [obey not] any gossip-monger going about with malicious gossip
Or [obey not] one who places obstacles in the way of good being done, transgressing with criminal intent
[And obey not] one who is cruel, besides being of no use to society
Just because he has wealth and sons
When Our Verses are recited to him, he says, "These are just ancient tales
Soon We will brand him on the nose [disgrace him]
We have indeed tried them as we tried the owners of the garden, who vowed to harvest its fruits the next morning
And they made no exception
And then a calamity from your Lord befell it [the garden] as they slept
And by morning it lay barren as if already harvested
And at dawn, they [the owners] called each other out
Reach your field early, to gather all your fruits
And so they proceeded, whispering to one another
Let no pauper enter the garden and trouble you today
And they went early, thinking they had the power to be firm
Then as they saw it, they said, "We must have lost our way
But, [no], utterly deprived are we
A moderate among them said, "Had I not asked you to invoke divine mercy and blessings
They said, "Glory be to our Lord! We have indeed been wrong
Then they started blaming one another
They said, "Alas for us, we did indeed transgress
May be our Lord will give us a garden better than this; we do indeed turn to Him now
Such is the punishment [in this life]! And the punishment of the life to come is certainly more severe, if only they knew
Indeed, for those who fear Allah, there will be the gardens of bliss with their Lord
Would We then treat the believers like the sinners
What is the matter with you? How ill you judge
Have you any book wherein you learn
That you will definitey have therein whatever you choose
Or do you have Our solemn pledges, binding upon Us till the Day of Resurrection, that you shall have whatever you order
Ask which of them will vouch for that [that there indeed are such solemn pledges divinely made]
Or do they worship gods besides Allah? Let them then come up with their other gods, if what they say be true
The Day the shin is laid bare, they will be called upon to prostrate themselves, but they will not be able to do so
Their glances will be downcast and ignominy shall cover them; they were called upon to prostrate [in this world], when they were safe and sound, [but they did not obey]
So leave to Me those who reject this Message. We shall rein them in, by degrees, from whence they know not
And I (Allah) give them a long rope. Indeed, My plan is fool-proof
Or do you demand some reward from them that would weigh them down with debt
Or, do they possess the knowledge of the unseen which they write down
So wait patiently for your Lord's decree! And be not like the companion of the fish, calling out in distress
Had not his Lord's favour taken hold of him [Prophet Jonas], he would have surely been flung away in disgrace upon that desolate shore
His Lord then chose him and made him one of the righteous men
And when those who suppress the truth hear the Admonition [Qur'aan], they would almost make you stumble with their eyes! And they say, "He is indeed mad
And it [Qur'aan] is not but an Admonition for all
The Inevitable
What is the Inevitable
And what do you know what the Inevitable is
The Thamood and the AAad denied possibility of the Striking Calamity happening
Then as for Thamood, they were destroyed by an overpowering blast!h
And as for the AAad, they were destroyed by a furious, violent storm
HE let it [storm] loose upon them for seven nights and eight days in succession. You would have seen the people there then lying prostrate, as though they were uprooted trunks of palm trees
Do you now see any trace of them
And Pharaoh and those before him and the people of the overturned habitations [the people of Lot] committed the same sin
And they followed not the Messenger of their Lord! So He seized them severely
When the water rose to great heights indeed, We bore you upon a floating vessel.h
So as to make it for you an event to remember, and so that an attentive ear commits it to memory
So when the Trumpet is blown with a single blow
And the earth and the mountains are lifted and then crushed at one stroke
On that Day shall the Event [the Hereafter, the Inevitable referred to in Verse above] come to pass
And the sky will be rent asunder, so it becomes loose that Day
And the angels will be at its edges. And eight of them will carry the Throne of your Lord that Day
That Day you shall be presented (before Allah) and no secret of yours shall remain hidden
He then, whose record will be given to him in his right hand, will say, "Here, read this record of mine
I did indeed expect that I would come face to face with my record
He shall then be living a life of bliss
In a lofty Garden
Clusters of its fruits will be within reach
Eat and drink to your satisfaction on account of what you did in the days gone by
And he, whose Record will be given to him in his left hand, will say, "Would that I had never been given my Record
And had I not come to know my account
Oh! Would that [death in the worldly life] be the end of me
My wealth has been of no use to me
My authority is gone from me
[Divine Order for him whose record is given in his left hand:] Seize him and shackle him
Then burn him in the Blazing Fire
Then tie him to a chain, seventy cubits long
He would not believe in Allah, the Almighty
And he would feel no urge to feed the poor
And so no friend for him here today
And no food except from discharged wastes
Eat it not but the sinners
But no! I swear by what you see
And by what you do not see
This [the Qur'aan] certainly indeed is a noble Messenger's [Angel's] Word
And not that of a poet! Little do you believe
Nor is it the word of a soothsayer! Little do you reflect
It is a reveation from the Lord of the Universe
And had he [the Prophet] ascribed to Us some of his own sayings
We would surely have seized from him by the right hand
And then severed from him the life vein
And none of you could wit old Us from doing this to him
And, indeed, it [the Qur'aan] is a divine Counsel for those who fear Allah
And We do indeed know that some among you deny this
And, indeed, it [the Qur'aan] is certainly a cause of regret for those who suppress the Truth
And certainly indeed it [the Qur'aan] is the absolute Truth
Chant, then, the name of your Lord, the Almighty
A questioner questions punishment that is bound to befall
Those who suppress the Truth. There is none to defend anyone
From Allah, Lord of the [many] ascents
The time taken by the angels and the Spirit to ascend to Him is fifty thousand years [of man's reckoning]
So, (O Prophet), be graciously patient [at the disbelievers' deliberate disbelief]
They do indeed see it [punishment] long in coming
And We see it near
That Day, the sky will be like molten metal
And the mountains will be like wool
And friend will not ask of friend
Although they would be able to see one another. The sinner would like to save himself from the punishment of that Day by offering (even) his children in ransom
And [he would offer] his spouse and his brother
And [he would offer] his kindred who sheltered him
And [he would offer] all all that is on the earth, if only he could thus save himself
But no! The fierce flame of Hell-fire it shall be
That would be stripping their scalds off
It [the Fire] would summon him who had turned away and retreated
And had amassed and hoarded
Man is indeed impatient by nature
When adversity touches him he bewails
And when prosperity touches him, he is begrudging
But those who pray are not [so impatient]
Those that are constant in their prayers
And those in whose wealth there is a known right
For those that beg and for those that are deprived
And [among those who are not impatient are] those who sincerely believe in the Day of Judgment
And those that fear the punishment of their Lord
— There is indeed no security against punishment of their Lord —
And those that guard their chastity
Except from their spouses or from those whom they rightfully possess. For indulging in sex with them, they are, of course, not to be blamed
But whoever seeks to go beyond that — those are the ones that go beyond limits
And [among those who are not impatient are] those who are true to their trusts and who keep their word
And those who firmly stand by their testimonies
And those who guard their prayer.h
All those shall be the honoured ones in Gardens of Paradise
And what is the matter with those that suppress the Truth that they rush to you
From the right and from the left, in groups
Does everyone of them hope to enter the Garden of Bliss [by following one's own man- made thought]
No, not at all! They know what We have created them from
By no means [can they enter the Garden of Bliss!] I swear by the Lord of the easts and the wests that We certainly are capable
Of replacing them by others better than they. And nothing can hinder Us
Leave them then to their vain talk and to their amusements, till they meet with the Day promised to them —
The Day on which they will come hastily out of their graves, as though they had to run towards their goals
Their eyes downcast and [their bodies] overwhelmed with disgrace! That is the Day they were promised
We did indeed send Noah to his people: "Warn your people before a painful punishment afflicts them
He said, "O my people! I am indeed sent to give you a plain warning
That you should worship Allah, and fear Him, and obey me
HE will forgive you some of your sins, and give you respite till an appointed time. When the Allah appointed time comes, it cannot be deferred, if only you knew
[Noah later] said, "My Lord! I have indeed preached to my people night and day
My preaching however has only drove them farther away
And, indeed, whenever I preached to them [to come to the Right Path] so that You might forgive them, they put their fingers into their ears, covered themselves up in their garments, grew obstinate, and became arrogant with false pride
And I did indeed preach to them loud and clear
And then I spoke to them in public; and I confided to them privately
And I said, `Ask your Lord to forgive you. He is indeed most forgiving
He will make the sky pour rain on you in abundance
And He will help you with wealth and children, and will make gardens for you, and will generate rivers for you
What is the matter with you that you do not attribute Grandeur to Allah
And He has surely created you [mankind] of diverse sorts and conditions
Do you not see how Allah has created seven heavens one over another
And He has made within these, the moon a light [reflected], and the sun, a [radiant] lamp
And Allah has grown you from the earth like a plant
Thereafter He will restore you to it [when you die]. And He will bring you out in resurrection
And Allah has made the earth spread out for you
So that you might thread thereon a network of spacious paths
Noah said, "My Lord! They have disobeyed me all along, and they follow one whose wealth and children increase nothing but their loss
And they plotted a great plot
And they told [their followers], "Abandon not your gods: abandon not Wadd, Suwa', Yaghuth, Ya'uq or Nasr
And they have verily led many astray. And [O Allah] increase nothing but their delusion for these wicked people
They [those wicked persons] were drowned because of their sins, and are doomed to enter the Fire [in the Hereafter]. And they found none to help them against Allah
And Noah prayed, "My Lord! Leave not any of those who suppress the Truth to inhabit on the earth
If You do indeed leave them, they will lead those who worship You astray, and will give birth to none but wicked and ingrate progeny
My Lord! Grant forgiveness to me, to my parents, to everyone who enters my house as a believer, and to all believing men and women. And grant increase in nothing buttheir destruction for the wicked people
Say (O Muhammad), "It is revealed to me that a group of the Jinn listened, and said, `We have heard an amazing Recital [Qur'aan]
It guides towards righteousness, so we believe in it. And we do not associate anyone else, in worship, with our Lord
And (we affirm) that He has neither wife nor son; exalted is the Majesty of our Lord
And that the foolish among us speak atrociously about Allah
And that we had thought mankind and jinn would not speak lies about Allah
And that individuals from mankind sought protection of individuals from the jinn, and so there was an increase in their evil disposition
And that they [men] thought, even as you [jinn] think, that Allah would not raise anyone from the dead
And that We did certainly touch [tried to reach out to] the heaven but found it replete with guards, strong and equipped with sharp, penetrating missiles of burning flame
And that we did sit on seats therein to listen. But, now, he who listens finds a flame in wait for him
And that we do not understand whether ill is intended for all those on the earth, or whether their Lord intends right guidance for them
And that some of us are righteous and some of us are not. We have been following different ways
And that we do think we cannot frustate Allah on the earth, nor can we escape from Him by fleeing
And that when we heard the guidance, we believed in it. And he who believes in his Lord, he fears neither loss nor any prevalence of evil
And that some among us have surrendered themselves to Allah and some are perverse. And whoso has surrendered to Allah, such have sought the right path
And those who are perverse, they are fuel for Hell-fire
And had they steadily stood by the right path, We would have given them plenty of water to drink (i.e. given them good peovision)
So that We may test them thereby. And he who turns away from the remembrance of his Lord, him He will make suffer ever-growing punishment
And [remember] that the Masajid [places of worship for believers] are for Allah, so pray to Allah and not to anyone else with Him
And that when the slave of Allah [Prophet Muhammad] stood up to pray to Him, they mobbed around him, almost stiflingly
Tell (them, O Muhammad), "I pray only to my Lord. And I pray not to anyone besides Him
Say, "I do indeed have no power either to hurt you or to put you on the right path
Say, "None indeed can protect me from Allah, nor can I find any provider of shelter besides Him
(I have no power) but to convey Notifications from Allah, and His Messages. And he who disobeys Allah and His Messenger, for him is Fire of Hell! Therein such people dwell for ever
Until they see what they are promised (the suppressors of Truth will remain deluded), but then they will come to know who is weak in support and less in number
Say, "I am unaware whether what is promised to you is near, or my Lord has set a distant time for it
He is the One Who knows the Unseen, and none else is privy to His [knowledge of] Unseen
Except those of His Messengers to whom He pleases [to convey any knowledge of the Unseen]. And then He appoints a guard to go before him and a guard behind him
So that He may know that they [Messengers] have truly conveyed the Messages of their Lord. He monitors all their doings from time to time, and He keeps account of all things one by one
O you who are wrapped up [against cold or to go to sleep]
Keep up at night, but a little
Half of it [night] or a little less
Or a little more, and put the Quran in proper order
Indeed, We are about to send down to you a message of great importance
Indeed, rising up at night is most suitable for impression and retention of words
[And] indeed, there are prolonged engagements for you during the day
And keep remembering name [attribute] of your Lord, and devote yourself to Him exclusively
He is the Lord of the east and the west! None is worthy of worship but He, so entrust all your affairs to His care
Be patient on what they say, and graciously leave them alone
And leave it to Me, and those who deny the Truth, living a life of comfort! And give them a little respite
Certainly indeed, We have for them heavy fetters and a blazing Fire
And food that chokes, and painful punishment
On the Day the earth and mountains shake, and the mountains become sand dunes crumbling down
We have indeed sent a Messenger to you who is a witness over you, just as We sent a Messenger to Pharoah
But Pharoah did not obey the Messenger, so We seized him with a violent seizure
If you deny the Day that will turn the children old, then how can you become righteous
The sky will break apart whereat, as His promise is fulfilled
This, indeed, is the divine Counsel. So let him who will, take the path to his Lord
Your Lord does indeed know that you are up for nearly two-thirds of the night, sometimes one-half of it and sometimes one-third of it, as do a group among your followers. And Allah determines the duration of the night and of the day. He knows that you will not be able to keep count of it [your night vigil], so He has turned to you in mercy. Read [study], then, as much of the Qur'aan as is easy for you. He knows that some among you would be sick and some others would be travelling in search of Allah's bounty [livelihood], and yet others would be fighting for the cause of Allah. So, read, then as much of it [Qur'aan] as is easy for you. And establish the prayer, pay the Zakaat, and give Allah a good loan. And the good deed you send in advance for your souls, you will find it with Allah. That is better and greater in reward. And seek Allah's forgiveness! Allah is indeed Forgiving, Merciful
O you folded up [in inactivity]
Arise and warn
And proclaim the greatness of your Lord
And keep your garments clean
And shun the dirt
And expect no [material] gain [for your own self]

By the night as it veils
And by the day as it unveils
And by the Power that created the male and the female
Indeed, your [mankind's] work is in divergent fields of activity
And, he who gave [things in Allah's Path] and feared Him
And stood firmly by what was good and right
For him shall We make things easy
And he who was miserly [in giving things in Allah's Path], and considered that he needed no divine help
And belied what was good and right
For him shall We make things difficult
And his wealth shall avail him not when he drops dead
It is certainly indeed for Us to give the guidance
And, certainly indeed, the Dominion over both the Hereafter and the present world is Ours
I then warn you of the flaming Fire
None shall burn in it [the Fire] but the wicked person
He who belies the Truth and turns away [from it]
And, he will be distanced from it [Fire] who fears Allah
He who spends his wealth [on others] to keep himself pure
— And he has none with him to be recompensed of favours received —
And he spends for nothing but to seek the pleasure of his Lord, the Most High
And such persons, certainly, shall in time be well-pleased
By the morning brightness
And by the night when it is still
Your Lord has not forsaken you [Prophet Muhammad], nor does He hate you
And, surely, the latter part [of your life] will be better for you than the earlier
And surely your Lord will give you [stability, security and authority], and then you will be happy
Did He not find you an orphan and give you shelter
Did He not find you wandering and give you guidance
Did He not find you poor and make you overcome poverty
Oppress not the orphan then
And scare not the beggar away
And recount then the bounty of your Lord
Have We not opened for you your head
And lifted your burden off you
Which [burden] weighed upon your back
And raised high the esteem, (in which) you (are held), for you
With every difficulty then, indeed, there is a way out
Indeed, with every difficulty there is a way out
So then, when you get free (of your difficulty or from your worldly task), rise up
And turn to your Lord in complete devotion and submission
By the fig and the olive
And by Mount Sinai
And by this city (Makkah) of peace
Surely, We created the human in the best of forms
Then We reverted the human to the lowest of the low
Except for those who believed and did righteous deeds. For them, an unending reward
What, then, do they deny you [O Prophet] for, post this Judgment [in Verses and above]
Is not Allah the Best of all judges
Read in the name of your Lord who creates —
Creates man from a clinging substance
Read and your Lord is most Liberal
Who taught by the pen —
Taught mankind what it knew not.h
Man, on the other hand, is certainly indeed prone to transgression
As he sees himself independent of any divine help
Indeed, to your Lord is the return
Have you seen him who forbids
A devotee when he prays
Do you see if he [the devotee] is on the right guidance
Or enjoins piety
[And] do you see if he [who forbids the devotee from praying] denies [Guidance] and turns away [from it]
Does he not know that Allah does indeed see [his wickedness]
Nay! If he does not desist, We will drag him by the forelock —
A lying, sinning forelock
Then let him call those who would help him
We will call the guardians of Hell
Nay! Obey him not, but prostrate and get near (to Allah)
We have indeed bestowed it [the Qur'aan] in the night of Divine Decree
And what do you understand what the night of divine Decree is
The night of divine Decree is better than a thousand months
The angels and the Spirit, by their Lord's leave, descend in that night with all His decrees
Peace it is, until the break of dawn
It could not be that those suppressing the Truth from among the people of the Book [Jews and Christians] and the polytheists were abandoned [by Allah], until there came to them the clear evidence
A Messenger from Allah, reciting scripts freed of all impurities
In it are rulings sound, clear and ever applicable
And those who have been given the divine Book [earlier] differed not but after the clear evidence had come to them
And they were enjoined not but to worship Allah, keeping their way of life exclusively for Him, turning away from all that was false; and to establish the prayer ; and to give the Zakaat. And this is the way of life sound, clear and ever applicable
Indeed, those who suppress the Truth from among the peoples who had been given the divine Book earlier and the polytheists — those will be in the fire of Hell, therein to abide: they are the worst of all creatures
Indeed, those who believe and do righteous deeds — it is they who are the best of all creatures
Their reward with their Lord: gardens of perpetual bliss, underneath which rivers flow, wherein to abide forever. Allah will be well-pleased with them, and they with Him. All this for him who fears his Lord
When the earth is shaken with its earthquake
And the earth brings out its burdens
And man wonders, "What is the matter with it
That Day it [the earth] will relate its stories
Because your Lord inspires it
That Day mankind will proceed in groups to be shown their deeds
Then whoever does [even] an atom's weight of good deed will see it
And whoever does [even] an atom's weight of bad deed will see it
By the chargers [horses ridden by warriors] panting
Then striking the sparks of fire
Then raiding at dawn
Then raising the dust therewith
Then charging into the midst collectively therewith
Man certainly indeed is ungrateful to his Lord
And he certainly indeed bears witness on this (that he is ungrateful)
And he is certainly indeed extremely fond of wealth
Does he not know that when the contents of the graves are taken out and examined
And that which was in (human) minds recovered
Their Lord shall have been well-aware of them, that Day
The Sudden Calamity
What is the Sudden Calamity
And what do you know what the Sudden Calamity is
It is a Day when mankind shall be like the scattered moths
And the mountains like fluffed up wool
That person, then, who weighs heavy [with good deeds] on the scales
[That person] shall have a pleasant life
And that person, who weighs light [because of bad deeds] on the scales
The Abyss then shall be his home
And what do you understand what it [the Abyss] is
A Fire intensely hot
The craving for more [worldly wealth and power] keeps you engrossed
Until you embrace the graves
Nay! You shall soon come to know
Nay again! You shall soon come to know
Nay, if you but knew with certain knowledge
You shall surely see the Hell
Then you shall surely see it with eye of certitude
And then, on that Day, you shall surely be questioned about the bounties you enjoyed
By the time
Indeed, mankind is surely in loss
But not those among them who believe and do good deeds, and exhort one another to Truth, and exhort one another to patience
Woe to everyone who taunts, slanders, or backbites others
Who hoards wealth and keeps on counting it [avariciously]
Thinking his wealth will last forever for him
Nay! He will surely be thrown into the Crushing Disaster
And what do you know what the Crushing Disaster is
It is the Fire kindled by Allah
That which would ride over human minds
It would be closing in on them from everyside
In extended columns
Have you not seen what your Lord did to the companions of the elephant
Did He not bring their plan to naught
And send upon them swarms of birds
Pelting them with stones of baked clay
And then making them look like chewed husk?h
For the welfare of the Qurays
Their welfare during winter and summer journeys [of their trading caravans]
So let them worship the Lord of this House
Who provided them food against hunger and security against fear
Have you seen the one who denies that there is a just divine system in place for mankind
Such a one it is that pushes the orphan away
And does not motivate others on feeding the poor
And, woe to those who pray —
Those who are neglectful of, and/or inattentive in, their Prayers
Those who show off
And refuse to give even trifling things to others
We have indeed given you the amplitude
So pray to your Lord and offer sacrifice for Him
Your enemy is the one to be cut off
Say, "O you who suppress the Truth
I worship not that which you worship
And you worship not Him Whom I worship
And I shall worship not that which you worship
And you worship not Him Whom I worship
For you your way of life and for me, mine
When Allah's help and the victory have come
And you see people entering Allah-ordained way of life for mankind, in large numbers
Then glorify your Lord with His praise, and seek His forgiveness. HE is indeed the One to accept repentance
Abu Lahab's hands are perished; and he too
His wealth and what he earned was of no avail to him
[In the life to come] he shall burn in a Fire of blazing flames
Along with his wife, carrier of (thorny) wood —
A rope of twisted strands in her neck
Say, "He is Allah, the One and Only
Allah, the eternal and independent Lord and Master on Whom everything in the Universe depends
He begets not nor is He begotten
And there is none comparable to Him
Say, "I seek refuge in Lord of the dawn
From the evil of what He has created
And from the evil of darkness when it sets in
And from the evil of those who blow on knots
And from the evil of the envious person when he envies
Say, "I seek refuge in the Lord of mankind
King of mankind
One Whom mankind should worship
From the evil of the temptations, doubts and suggestions of the stealthy whisperer
— One who puts the evil things in minds of mankind —
From among the jinn and mankind
